Honestly these guys are so shit at their jobs. Candy below 150* F can be touched because candy is an insulator of heat, which means it doesn't burn your skin quickly when touched due to its low ability to transfer heat. Using gloves can ruin the candy because the rubber in gloves can create a chemical reaction which poisons candy to poison similar to the likes of mercury. (Take it from a guy who started a candy company from the ground up.)

That method of putting the panda face together is very similar to how you make buttons and beads out of Fimo or Sculpty polymer clay. You place certain strips of colors together, assemble them and wrap the last color around the whole log and roll the heck out of it and compress the design and cut them cross wise then bake to harden them.

Just wondering, why do you use white colouring?  If you take the plain candy and stretch it over and over by hand or on a candy hook it will take on tiny air bubbles and turn from a translucent yellow to an opaque white.
